text-fd-secondary-foreground hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground px-2 py-1.5 text-xs gap-2">Open<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-chevron-down size-3.5 text-fd-muted-foreground" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m6 9 6 6 6-6"></path></svg></button></div></div><p class="mb-2 text-lg text-fd-muted-foreground">How to configure index functionality and add full text indexes</p><div class="prose flex-1"><p>Prisma ORM allows configuration of database indexes, unique constraints and primary key constraints. Full text indexes in MySQL and MongoDB are available through the <code>fullTextIndex</code> preview feature using the <code>@@fulltext</code> attribute.</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="index-configuration"><a data-card="" href="#index-configuration" class="peer">Index configuration</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>You can configure indexes, unique constraints, and primary key constraints with the following attribute arguments:</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>The <a href="#configuring-the-length-of-indexes-with-length-mysql"><code>length</code> argument</a> allows you to specify a maximum length for the subpart of the value to be indexed on <code>String</code> and <code>Bytes</code> types</p>
<ul>
<li>Available on the <code>@id</code>, <code>@@id</code>, <code>@unique</code>, <code>@@unique</code> and <code>@@index</code> attributes</li>
<li>MySQL only</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p>The <a href="#configuring-the-index-sort-order-with-sort"><code>sort</code> argument</a> allows you to specify the order that the entries of the constraint or index are stored in the database</p>
<ul>
<li>Available on the <code>@unique</code>, <code>@@unique</code> and <code>@@index</code> attributes in all databases, and on the <code>@id</code> and <code>@@id</code> attributes in SQL Server</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p>The <a href="#configuring-the-access-type-of-indexes-with-type-postgresql"><code>type</code> argument</a> allows you to support index access methods other than PostgreSQL&#x27;s default <code>BTree</code> access method</p>
<ul>
<li>Available on the <code>@@index</code> attribute</li>
<li>PostgreSQL only</li>
<li>Supported index access methods: <code>Hash</code>, <code>Gist</code>, <code>Gin</code>, <code>SpGist</code> and <code>Brin</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p>The <a href="#configuring-if-indexes-are-clustered-or-non-clustered-with-clustered-sql-server"><code>clustered</code> argument</a> allows you to configure whether a constraint or index is clustered or non-clustered</p>
<ul>
<li>Available on the <code>@id</code>, <code>@@id</code>, <code>@unique</code>, <code>@@unique</code> and <code>@@index</code> attributes</li>
<li>SQL Server only</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p>The <a href="#configuring-the-name-of-indexes-with-map"><code>map</code> argument</a> allows you to specify a custom name for the index or constraint in the underlying database</p>
<ul>
<li>Available on the <code>@id</code>, <code>@@id</code>, <code>@unique</code>, <code>@@unique</code> and <code>@@index</code> attributes</li>
<li>Supported in all databases</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="configuring-the-length-of-indexes-with-length-mysql"><a data-card="" href="#configuring-the-length-of-indexes-with-length-mysql" class="peer">Configuring the length of indexes with <code>length</code> (MySQL)</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>The <code>length</code> argument is specific to MySQL and allows you to define indexes and constraints on columns of <code>String</code> and <code>Byte</code> types. For these types, MySQL requires you to specify a maximum length for the subpart of the value to be indexed in cases where the full value would exceed MySQL&#x27;s limits for index sizes. See <a href="https://dev.mysql.com/doc/refman/8.0/en/innodb-limits.html" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">the MySQL documentation</a> for more details.</p>
<p>The <code>length</code> argument is available on the <code>@id</code>, <code>@@id</code>, <code>@unique</code>, <code>@@unique</code> and <code>@@index</code> attributes.</p>
<p>As an example, the following data model declares an <code>id</code> field with a maximum length of 3000 characters:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="flex text-fd-muted-foreground items-center gap-2 h-9.5 border-b px-4"><div class="[&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M21.8068 18.2848L13.5528.7565c-.207-.4382-.639-.7273-1.1286-.7541-.5023-.0293-.9523.213-1.2062.6253L2.266 15.1271c-.2773.4518-.2718 1.0091.0158 1.4555l4.3759 6.7786c.2608.4046.7127.6388 1.1823.6388.1332 0 .267-.0188.3987-.0577l12.7019-3.7568c.3891-.1151.7072-.3904.8737-.7553s.1633-.7828-.0075-1.1454zm-1.8481.7519L9.1814 22.2242c-.3292.0975-.6448-.1873-.5756-.5194l3.8501-18.4386c.072-.3448.5486-.3996.699-.0803l7.1288 15.138c.1344.2856-.019.6224-.325.7128z" fill="currentColor" /></svg></div><figcaption class="flex-1 truncate">schema.prisma</figcaption><div class="empty:hidden -me-2"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">model</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Id</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  id </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">String</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> @id</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> @db.VarChar</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">3000</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>This is not valid in MySQL because it exceeds MySQL&#x27;s index storage limit and therefore Prisma ORM rejects the data model. The generated SQL would be rejected by the database.</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">CREATE</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> TABLE</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> `</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">Id</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">` (</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">  `id`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> VARCHAR</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">3000</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">PRIMARY KEY</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>The <code>length</code> argument allows you to specify that only a subpart of the <code>id</code> value represents the primary key. In the example below, the first 100 characters are used:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" class="[&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M21.8068 18.2848L13.5528.7565c-.207-.4382-.639-.7273-1.1286-.7541-.5023-.0293-.9523.213-1.2062.6253L2.266 15.1271c-.2773.4518-.2718 1.0091.0158 1.4555l4.3759 6.7786c.2608.4046.7127.6388 1.1823.6388.1332 0 .267-.0188.3987-.0577l12.7019-3.7568c.3891-.1151.7072-.3904.8737-.7553s.1633-.7828-.0075-1.1454zm-1.8481.7519L9.1814 22.2242c-.3292.0975-.6448-.1873-.5756-.5194l3.8501-18.4386c.072-.3448.5486-.3996.699-.0803l7.1288 15.138c.1344.2856-.019.6224-.325.7128z" fill="currentColor" /></svg></div><figcaption class="flex-1 truncate">schema.prisma</figcaption><div class="empty:hidden -me-2"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">model</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Id</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  id </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">String</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> @id</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">length</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">100</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">@db.VarChar</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">3000</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>Prisma Migrate is able to create constraints and indexes with the <code>length</code> argument if specified in your data model. This means that you can create indexes and constraints on values of Prisma schema type <code>Byte</code> and <code>String</code>. If you don&#x27;t specify the argument the index is treated as covering the full value as before.</p>
<p>Introspection will fetch these limits where they are present in your existing database. This allows Prisma ORM to support indexes and constraints that were previously suppressed and results in better support of MySQL databases utilizing this feature.</p>
<p>The <code>length</code> argument can also be used on compound primary keys, using the <code>@@id</code> attribute, as in the example below:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="flex text-fd-muted-foreground items-center gap-2 h-9.5 border-b px-4"><div class="[&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M21.8068 18.2848L13.5528.7565c-.207-.4382-.639-.7273-1.1286-.7541-.5023-.0293-.9523.213-1.2062.6253L2.266 15.1271c-.2773.4518-.2718 1.0091.0158 1.4555l4.3759 6.7786c.2608.4046.7127.6388 1.1823.6388.1332 0 .267-.0188.3987-.0577l12.7019-3.7568c.3891-.1151.7072-.3904.8737-.7553s.1633-.7828-.0075-1.1454zm-1.8481.7519L9.1814 truncate">schema.prisma</figcaption><div class="empty:hidden -me-2"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">model</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> CompoundId</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  id_1 </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">String</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> @db.VarChar</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">3000</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  id_2 </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">String</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> @db.VarChar</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">3000</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">  @@id</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">([</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">id_1</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">length</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">100</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">), </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">id_2</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">length</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">10</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)])</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>A similar syntax can be used for the <code>@@unique</code> and <code>@@index</code> attributes.</p>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="configuring-the-index-sort-order-with-sort"><a data-card="" href="#configuring-the-index-sort-order-with-sort" class="peer">Configuring the index sort order with <code>sort</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>The <code>sort</code> argument allows you to specify the order that the entries of the index or constraint are stored in the database. This can have an effect on whether the database is able to use an index for specific queries. The behavior and support varies by database:</p>
<ul>
<li>In MySQL/MariaDB, you can specify sort order (<code>ASC</code>/<code>DESC</code>) directly in unique constraints and indexes</li>
<li>In PostgreSQL, sort order can only be specified on indexes, not on unique constraints</li>
<li>In SQL Server, sort order is supported on all constraints and indexes including <code>@id</code> and <code>@@id</code></li>
</ul>
<p>For example, in MySQL/MariaDB, the following table using a descending unique constraint:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">CREATE</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> TABLE</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> `</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">Unique</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">` (</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">  `unique`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> INT</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  CONSTRAINT</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> `Unique_unique_key`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> UNIQUE</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">`unique`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> DESC</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>would be introspected as</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="flex text-fd-muted-foreground items-center gap-2 h-9.5 border-b px-4"><div class="[&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M21.8068 18.2848L13.5528.7565c-.207-.4382-.639-.7273-1.1286-.7541-.5023-.0293-.9523.213-1.2062.6253L2.266 15.1271c-.2773.4518-.2718 1.0091.0158 1.4555l4.3759 6.7786c.2608.4046.7127.6388 1.1823.6388.1332 0 .267-.0188.3987-.0577l12.7019-3.7568c.3891-.1151.7072-.3904.8737-.7553s.1633-.7828-.0075-1.1454zm-1.8481.7519L9.1814 22.2242c-.3292.0975-.6448-.1873-.5756-.5194l3.8501-18.4386c.072-.3448.5486-.3996.699-.0803l7.1288 15.138c.1344.2856-.019.6224-.325.7128z" fill="currentColor" /></svg></div><figcaption class="flex-1 truncate">schema.prisma</figcaption><div class="empty:hidden -me-2"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">model</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Unique</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  unique </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> @unique</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">sort</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Desc</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>Note that in PostgreSQL, while you cannot specify sort order on unique constraints directly, you can create a unique index with a sort order that will enforce uniqueness:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">-- PostgreSQL approach</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">CREATE</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> UNIQUE INDEX</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> &quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">unique_index_desc</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&quot; </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">ON</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;Unique&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;unique&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> DESC</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>The <code>sort</code> argument can also be used on compound indexes:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="flex text-fd-muted-foreground items-center gap-2 h-9.5 border-b px-4"><div class="[&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M21.8068 18.2848L13.5528.7565c-.207-.4382-.639-.7273-1.1286-.7541-.5023-.0293-.9523.213-1.2062.6253L2.266 15.1271c-.2773.4518-.2718 1.0091.0158 1.4555l4.3759 6.7786c.2608.4046.7127.6388 1.1823.6388.1332 0 .267-.0188.3987-.0577l12.7019-3.7568c.3891-.1151.7072-.3904.8737-.7553s.1633-.7828-.0075-1.1454zm-1.8481.7519L9.1814 22.2242c-.3292.0975-.6448-.1873-.5756-.5194l3.8501-18.4386c.072-.3448.5486-.3996.699-.0803l7.1288 15.138c.1344.2856-.019.6224-.325.7128z" fill="currentColor" /></svg></div><figcaption class="flex-1 truncate">schema.prisma</figcaption><div class="empty:hidden -me-2"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">model</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> CompoundUnique</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  unique_1 </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Int</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  unique_2 </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Int</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">  @@unique</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">([</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">unique_1</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">sort</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Desc</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">), </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">unique_2</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">])</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="example-using-sort-and-length-together"><a data-card="" href="#example-using-sort-and-length-together" class="peer">Example: using <code>sort</code> and <code>length</code> together</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>The following example demonstrates the use of the <code>sort</code> and <code>length</code> arguments to configure indexes and constraints for a <code>Post</code> model:</p>

class="[&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M21.8068 18.2848L13.5528.7565c-.207-.4382-.639-.7273-1.1286-.7541-.5023-.0293-.9523.213-1.2062.6253L2.266 15.1271c-.2773.4518-.2718 1.0091.0158 1.4555l4.3759 6.7786c.2608.4046.7127.6388 1.1823.6388.1332 0 .267-.0188.3987-.0577l12.7019-3.7568c.3891-.1151.7072-.3904.8737-.7553s.1633-.7828-.0075-1.1454zm-1.8481.7519L9.1814 22.2242c-.3292.0975-.6448-.1873-.5756-.5194l3.8501-18.4386c.072-.3448.5486-.3996.699-.0803l7.1288 15.138c.1344.2856-.019.6224-.325.7128z" fill="currentColor" /></svg></div><figcaption class="flex-1 data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" <span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  title      </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">String</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">   @db.VarChar</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">300</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  abstract   </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">String</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">   @db.VarChar</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">3000</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  slug       </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">String</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">   @unique</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">sort</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Desc</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">length</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">42</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">@db.VarChar</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">3000</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  author     </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">String</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  created_at </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">DateTime</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">  @@id</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">([</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">title</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">length</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">100</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">sort</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Desc</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">), </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">abstract</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">length</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">10</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)])</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">  @@index</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">([</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">author</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">created_at</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">sort</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Desc</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)])</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="configuring-the-access-type-of-indexes-with-type-postgresql"><a data-card="" href="#configuring-the-access-type-of-indexes-with-type-postgresql" class="peer">Configuring the access type of indexes with <code>type</code> (PostgreSQL)</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>The <code>type</code> argument is available for configuring the index type in PostgreSQL with the <code>@@index</code> attribute. The index access methods available are <code>Hash</code>, <code>Gist</code>, <code>Gin</code>, <code>SpGist</code> and <code>Brin</code>, as well as the default <code>BTree</code> index access method.</p>
<h4 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="hash"><a data-card="" href="#hash" class="peer">Hash</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h4>
<p>The <code>Hash</code> type will store the index data in a format that is much faster to search and insert, and that will use less disk space. However, only the <code>=</code> and <code>&lt;&gt;</code> comparisons can use the index, so other comparison operators such as <code>&lt;</code> and <code>&gt;</code> will be much slower with <code>Hash</code> than when using the default <code>BTree</code> type.</p>
<p>As an example, the following model adds an index with a <code>type</code> of <code>Hash</code> to the <code>value</code> field:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="flex text-fd-muted-foreground items-center gap-2 h-9.5 border-b px-4"><div class="[&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M21.8068 18.2848L13.5528.7565c-.207-.4382-.639-.7273-1.1286-.7541-.5023-.0293-.9523.213-1.2062.6253L2.266 15.1271c-.2773.4518-.2718 1.0091.0158 1.4555l4.3759 6.7786c.2608.4046.7127.6388 1.1823.6388.1332 0 .267-.0188.3987-.0577l12.7019-3.7568c.3891-.1151.7072-.3904.8737-.7553s.1633-.7828-.0075-1.1454zm-1.8481.7519L9.1814 22.2242c-.3292.0975-.6448-.1873-.5756-.5194l3.8501-18.4386c.072-.3448.5486-.3996.699-.0803l7.1288 15.138c.1344.2856-.019.6224-.325.7128z" fill="currentColor" /></svg></div><figcaption class="flex-1 truncate">schema.prisma</figcaption><div class="empty:hidden -me-2"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">model</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Example</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  id    </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> @id</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  value </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Int</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">  @@index</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">([</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">value</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">], </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Hash</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>This translates to the following SQL commands:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">CREATE</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> TABLE</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> &quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">Example</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&quot; (</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  id </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">INT</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> PRIMARY KEY</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  value</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> INT</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> NOT NULL</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">CREATE</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> INDEX</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> &quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">Example_value_idx</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&quot; </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">ON</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;Example&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> USING</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> HASH</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">value</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<h4 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="generalized-inverted-index-gin"><a data-card="" href="#generalized-inverted-index-gin" class="peer">Generalized Inverted Index (GIN)</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h4>
<p>The GIN index stores composite values, such as arrays or <code>JsonB</code> data. This is useful for speeding up querying whether one object is part of another object. It is commonly used for full-text searches.</p>
<p>An indexed field can define the operator class, which defines the operators handled by the index.</p>
<div role="alert" class="relative w-full rounded-md border p-4 gap-3 text-sm [&amp;&gt;svg]:left-4 [&amp;&gt;svg]:top-4 [&amp;&gt;svg]:w-5 [&amp;&gt;svg]:h-5 alert-admonition flex items-start [&amp;&gt;i]:mt-0.5 bg-background-warning border-none text-foreground-warning [&amp;&gt;svg]:text-foreground-warning"><i class="fa-duotone fa-solid fa-circle-exclamation"></i><div class="[&amp;&gt;*]:first:mt-0 [&amp;&gt;*]:last:mb-0 [&amp; strong]:text-inherit"><p>Indexes using a function (such as <code>to_tsvector</code>) to determine the indexed value are not yet supported by Prisma ORM. Indexes defined in this way will not be visible with <code>prisma db pull</code>.</p></div></div>
<p>As an example, the following model adds a <code>Gin</code> index to the <code>value</code> field, with <code>JsonbPathOps</code> as the class of operators allowed to use the index:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="flex text-fd-muted-foreground items-center gap-2 h-9.5 border-b px-4"><div class="[&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M21.8068 18.2848L13.5528.7565c-.207-.4382-.639-.7273-1.1286-.7541-.5023-.0293-.9523.213-1.2062.6253L2.266 15.1271c-.2773.4518-.2718 1.0091.0158 1.4555l4.3759 6.7786c.2608.4046.7127.6388 1.1823.6388.1332 0 .267-.0188.3987-.0577l12.7019-3.7568c.3891-.1151.7072-.3904.8737-.7553s.1633-.7828-.0075-1.1454zm-1.8481.7519L9.1814 22.2242c-.3292.0975-.6448-.1873-.5756-.5194l3.8501-18.4386c.072-.3448.5486-.3996.699-.0803l7.1288 15.138c.1344.2856-.019.6224-.325.7128z" fill="currentColor" /></svg></div><figcaption class="flex-1 truncate">schema.prisma</figcaption><div class="empty:hidden -me-2"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">model</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Example</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  id    </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">  @id</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  value </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Json</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">  //    ^ field type matching the operator class</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">  @@index</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">([</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">value</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">ops</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">JsonbPathOps</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)], </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Gin</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">  //                  ^ operator class      ^ index type</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>This translates to the following SQL commands:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">CREATE</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> TABLE</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> &quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">Example</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&quot; (</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  id </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">INT</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> PRIMARY KEY</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  value</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> JSONB </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">NOT NULL</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">CREATE</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> INDEX</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> &quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">Example_value_idx</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&quot; </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">ON</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;Example&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> USING</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> GIN (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">value</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> jsonb_path_ops);</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>As part of the <code>JsonbPathOps</code> the <code>@&gt;</code> operator is handled by the index, speeding up queries such as <code>value @&gt; &#x27;{&quot;foo&quot;: 2}&#x27;</code>.</p>
<h5 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="supported-operator-classes-for-gin"><a data-card="" href="#supported-operator-classes-for-gin" class="peer">Supported Operator Classes for GIN</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h5>
<p>Prisma ORM generally supports operator classes provided by PostgreSQL in versions 10 and later. If the operator class requires the field type to be of a type Prisma ORM does not yet support, using the <code>raw</code> function with a string input allows you to use these operator classes without validation.</p>
<p>The default operator class (marked with ✅) can be omitted from the index definition.</p>
<div class="relative w-full overflow-auto"><table class="w-full caption-bottom text-sm"><thead class="[&amp;_tr]:border-b"><tr class="border-b transition-colors hover:bg-muted/50 data-[state=selected]:bg-muted"><th class="h-10 px-3 py-4 text-left align-middle font-medium text-foreground-neutral [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] only:text-xl bg-background-neutral-weaker">Operator class</th><th class="h-10 px-3 py-4 text-left align-middle font-medium text-foreground-neutral [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] only:text-xl bg-background-neutral-weaker">Allowed field type (native types)</th><th class="h-10 px-3 py-4 text-left align-middle font-medium text-foreground-neutral [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] only:text-xl bg-background-neutral-weaker">Default</th><th class="h-10 px-3 py-4 text-left align-middle font-medium text-foreground-neutral [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] only:text-xl bg-background-neutral-weaker">Other</th></tr></thead><tbody class="[&amp;_tr:last-child]:border-0"><tr class="border-b transition-colors hover:bg-muted/50 data-[state=selected]:bg-muted"><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"><code>ArrayOps</code></td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default">Any array</td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default">✅</td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default">Also available in CockroachDB</td></tr><tr class="border-b transition-colors hover:bg-muted/50 data-[state=selected]:bg-muted"><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"><code>JsonbOps</code></td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"><code>Json</code> (<code>@db.JsonB</code>)</td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default">✅</td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default">Also available in CockroachDB</td></tr><tr class="border-b transition-colors hover:bg-muted/50 data-[state=selected]:bg-muted"><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"><code>JsonbPathOps</code></td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"><code>Json</code> (<code>@db.JsonB</code>)</td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"></td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"></td></tr><tr class="border-b transition-colors hover:bg-muted/50 data-[state=selected]:bg-muted"><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"><code>raw(&quot;other&quot;)</code></td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"></td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"></td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"></td></tr></tbody></table></div>
<p>Read more about built-in operator classes in the <a href="https://www.postgresql.org/docs/14/gin-builtin-opclasses.html" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">official PostgreSQL documentation</a>.</p>
<h5 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="cockroachdb"><a data-card="" href="#cockroachdb" class="peer">CockroachDB</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h5>
<p>GIN and BTree are the only index types supported by CockroachDB. The operator classes marked to work with CockroachDB are the only ones allowed on that database and supported by Prisma ORM. The operator class cannot be defined in the Prisma Schema Language: the <code>ops</code> argument is not necessary or allowed on CockroachDB.</p>
<h4 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="generalized-search-tree-gist"><a data-card="" href="#generalized-search-tree-gist" class="peer">Generalized Search Tree (GiST)</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h4>
<p>The GiST index type is used for implementing indexing schemes for user-defined types. By default there are not many direct uses for GiST indexes, but for example the B-Tree index type is built using a GiST index.</p>
<p>As an example, the following model adds a <code>Gist</code> index to the <code>value</code> field with <code>InetOps</code> as the operators that will be using the index:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="flex text-fd-muted-foreground items-center gap-2 h-9.5 border-b px-4"><div class="[&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M21.8068 18.2848L13.5528.7565c-.207-.4382-.639-.7273-1.1286-.7541-.5023-.0293-.9523.213-1.2062.6253L2.266 15.1271c-.2773.4518-.2718 1.0091.0158 1.4555l4.3759 6.7786c.2608.4046.7127.6388 1.1823.6388.1332 0 .267-.0188.3987-.0577l12.7019-3.7568c.3891-.1151.7072-.3904.8737-.7553s.1633-.7828-.0075-1.1454zm-1.8481.7519L9.1814 22.2242c-.3292.0975-.6448-.1873-.5756-.5194l3.8501-18.4386c.072-.3448.5486-.3996.699-.0803l7.1288 15.138c.1344.2856-.019.6224-.325.7128z" fill="currentColor" /></svg></div><figcaption class="flex-1 data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">model</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Example</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  id    </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">    @id</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">  //           ^ native type matching the operator class</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">  //                                   ^ index type</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">  //                  ^ operator class</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">  @@index</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">([</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">value</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">ops</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">InetOps</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)], </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Gist</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>This translates to the following SQL commands:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">CREATE</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> TABLE</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> &quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">Example</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&quot; (</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  id </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">INT</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> PRIMARY KEY</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  value</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> INET</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> NOT NULL</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">CREATE</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> INDEX</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> &quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">Example_value_idx</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&quot; </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">ON</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;Example&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> USING</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> GIST (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">value</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> inet_ops);</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>Queries comparing IP addresses, such as <code>value &gt; &#x27;10.0.0.2&#x27;</code>, will use the index.</p>
<h5 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="supported-operator-classes-for-gist"><a data-card="" href="#supported-operator-classes-for-gist" class="peer">Supported Operator Classes for GiST</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h5>
<p>Prisma ORM generally supports operator classes provided by PostgreSQL in versions 10 and later. If the operator class requires the field type to be of a type Prisma ORM does not yet support, using the <code>raw</code> function with a string input allows you to use these operator classes without validation.</p>
<div class="relative w-full overflow-auto"><table class="w-full caption-bottom text-sm"><thead class="[&amp;_tr]:border-b"><tr class="border-b transition-colors hover:bg-muted/50 data-[state=selected]:bg-muted"><th class="h-10 px-3 py-4 text-left align-middle font-medium text-foreground-neutral [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] only:text-xl bg-background-neutral-weaker">Operator class</th><th class="h-10 px-3 py-4 text-left align-middle font-medium text-foreground-neutral [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] only:text-xl bg-background-neutral-weaker">Allowed field type (allowed native types)</th></tr></thead><tbody class="[&amp;_tr:last-child]:border-0"><tr class="border-b transition-colors hover:bg-muted/50 data-[state=selected]:bg-muted"><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"><code>InetOps</code></td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"><code>String</code> (<code>@db.Inet</code>)</td></tr><tr class="border-b transition-colors hover:bg-muted/50 data-[state=selected]:bg-muted"><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"><code>raw(&quot;other&quot;)</code></td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"></td></tr></tbody></table></div>
<p>Read more about built-in operator classes in the <a href="https://www.postgresql.org/docs/14/gist-builtin-opclasses.html" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">official PostgreSQL documentation</a>.</p>
<h4 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="space-partitioned-gist-sp-gist"><a data-card="" href="#space-partitioned-gist-sp-gist" class="peer">Space-Partitioned GiST (SP-GiST)</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h4>
<p>The SP-GiST index is a good choice for many different non-balanced data structures. If the query matches the partitioning rule, it can be very fast.</p>
<p>As with GiST, SP-GiST is important as a building block for user-defined types, allowing implementation of custom search operators directly with the database.</p>
<p>As an example, the following model adds a <code>SpGist</code> index to the <code>value</code> field with <code>TextOps</code> as the operators using the index:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="flex text-fd-muted-foreground items-center gap-2 h-9.5 border-b px-4"><div class="[&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M21.8068 18.2848L13.5528.7565c-.207-.4382-.639-.7273-1.1286-.7541-.5023-.0293-.9523.213-1.2062.6253L2.266 15.1271c-.2773.4518-.2718
