22.2242c-.3292.0975-.6448-.1873-.5756-.5194l3.8501-18.4386c.072-.3448.5486-.3996.699-.0803l7.1288 15.138c.1344.2856-.019.6224-.325.7128z" fill="currentColor" /></svg></div><figcaption class="flex-1 truncate">schema.prisma</figcaption><div class="empty:hidden -me-2"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">model</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Example</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  id    </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">    @id</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  value </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">String</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">  //    ^ field type matching the operator class</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">  @@index</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">([</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">value</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">], </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">SpGist</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">  //                     ^ index type</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">  //       ^ using the default ops: TextOps</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>This translates to the following SQL commands:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">CREATE</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> TABLE</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> &quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">Example</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&quot; (</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  id </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">INT</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> PRIMARY KEY</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  value</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> TEXT</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> NOT NULL</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">CREATE</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> INDEX</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> &quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">Example_value_idx</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&quot; </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">ON</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;Example&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> USING</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> SPGIST (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">value</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>Queries such as <code>value LIKE &#x27;something%&#x27;</code> will be sped up by the index.</p>
<h5 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="supported-operator-classes-for-sp-gist"><a data-card="" href="#supported-operator-classes-for-sp-gist" class="peer">Supported Operator Classes for SP-GiST</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h5>
<p>Prisma ORM generally supports operator classes provided by PostgreSQL in versions 10 and later. If the operator class requires the field type to be of a type Prisma ORM does not yet support, using the <code>raw</code> function with a string input allows you to use these operator classes without validation.</p>
<p>The default operator class (marked with ✅) can be omitted from the index definition.</p>
<div class="relative w-full overflow-auto"><table class="w-full caption-bottom text-sm"><thead class="[&amp;_tr]:border-b"><tr class="border-b transition-colors hover:bg-muted/50 data-[state=selected]:bg-muted"><th class="h-10 px-3 py-4 text-left align-middle font-medium text-foreground-neutral [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] only:text-xl bg-background-neutral-weaker">Operator class</th><th class="h-10 px-3 py-4 text-left align-middle font-medium text-foreground-neutral [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] only:text-xl bg-background-neutral-weaker">Allowed field type (native types)</th><th class="h-10 px-3 py-4 text-left align-middle font-medium text-foreground-neutral [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] only:text-xl bg-background-neutral-weaker">Default</th><th class="h-10 px-3 py-4 text-left align-middle font-medium text-foreground-neutral [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] only:text-xl bg-background-neutral-weaker">Supported PostgreSQL versions</th></tr></thead><tbody class="[&amp;_tr:last-child]:border-0"><tr class="border-b transition-colors hover:bg-muted/50 data-[state=selected]:bg-muted"><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"><code>InetOps</code></td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"><code>String</code> (<code>@db.Inet</code>)</td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default">✅</td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default">10+</td></tr><tr class="border-b transition-colors hover:bg-muted/50 data-[state=selected]:bg-muted"><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"><code>TextOps</code></td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"><code>String</code> (<code>@db.Text</code>, <code>@db.VarChar</code>)</td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default">✅</td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"></td></tr><tr class="border-b transition-colors hover:bg-muted/50 data-[state=selected]:bg-muted"><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"><code>raw(&quot;other&quot;)</code></td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"></td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"></td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"></td></tr></tbody></table></div>
<p>Read more about built-in operator classes from <a href="https://www.postgresql.org/docs/14/spgist-builtin-opclasses.html" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">official PostgreSQL documentation</a>.</p>
<h4 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="block-range-index-brin"><a data-card="" href="#block-range-index-brin" class="peer">Block Range Index (BRIN)</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h4>
<p>The BRIN index type is useful if you have lots of data that does not change after it is inserted, such as date and time values. If your data is a good fit for the index, it can store large datasets in a minimal space.</p>
<p>As an example, the following model adds a <code>Brin</code> index to the <code>value</code> field with <code>Int4BloomOps</code> as the operators that will be using the index:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="flex text-fd-muted-foreground items-center gap-2 h-9.5 border-b px-4"><div class="[&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M21.8068 18.2848L13.5528.7565c-.207-.4382-.639-.7273-1.1286-.7541-.5023-.0293-.9523.213-1.2062.6253L2.266 15.1271c-.2773.4518-.2718 1.0091.0158 1.4555l4.3759 6.7786c.2608.4046.7127.6388 1.1823.6388.1332 0 .267-.0188.3987-.0577l12.7019-3.7568c.3891-.1151.7072-.3904.8737-.7553s.1633-.7828-.0075-1.1454zm-1.8481.7519L9.1814 22.2242c-.3292.0975-.6448-.1873-.5756-.5194l3.8501-18.4386c.072-.3448.5486-.3996.699-.0803l7.1288 15.138c.1344.2856-.019.6224-.325.7128z" fill="currentColor" /></svg></div><figcaption class="flex-1 truncate">schema.prisma</figcaption><div class="empty:hidden -me-2"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">model</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Example</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  id    </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> @id</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  value </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Int</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">  //    ^ field type matching the operator class</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">  @@index</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">([</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">value</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">ops</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Int4BloomOps</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)], </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Brin</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">  //                  ^ operator class      ^ index type</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>This translates to the following SQL commands:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">CREATE</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> TABLE</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> &quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">Example</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&quot; (</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  id </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">INT</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> PRIMARY KEY</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  value</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> INT4 </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">NOT NULL</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">CREATE</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> INDEX</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> &quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">Example_value_idx</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&quot; </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">ON</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;Example&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> USING</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> BRIN (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">value</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> int4_bloom_ops);</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>Queries like <code>value = 2</code> will now use the index, which uses a fraction of the space used by the <code>BTree</code> or <code>Hash</code> indexes.</p>
<h5 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="supported-operator-classes-for-brin"><a data-card="" href="#supported-operator-classes-for-brin" class="peer">Supported Operator Classes for BRIN</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h5>
<p>Prisma ORM generally supports operator classes provided by PostgreSQL in versions 10 and later, and some supported operators are only available from PostgreSQL versions 14 and later. If the operator class requires the field type to be of a type Prisma ORM does not yet support, using the <code>raw</code> function with a string input allows you to use these operator classes without validation.</p>
<p>The default operator class (marked with ✅) can be omitted from the index definition.</p>

only:text-xl bg-background-neutral-weaker">Operator class</th><th class="h-10 px-3 py-4 text-left align-middle font-medium text-foreground-neutral [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 text-foreground-neutral [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] only:text-xl bg-background-neutral-weaker">Default</th><th class="h-10 px-3 py-4 text-left align-middle font-medium text-foreground-neutral [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] only:text-xl bg-background-neutral-weaker">Supported PostgreSQL versions</th></tr></thead><tbody class="[&amp;_tr:last-child]:border-0"><tr class="border-b transition-colors hover:bg-muted/50 data-[state=selected]:bg-muted"><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"><code>BitMinMaxOps</code></td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"><code>String</code> (<code>@db.Bit</code>)</td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 <p>Read more about built-in operator classes in the <a href="https://www.postgresql.org/docs/14/brin-builtin-opclasses.html" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">official PostgreSQL documentation</a>.</p>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="configuring-if-indexes-are-clustered-or-non-clustered-with-clustered-sql-server"><a data-card="" href="#configuring-if-indexes-are-clustered-or-non-clustered-with-clustered-sql-server" class="peer">Configuring if indexes are clustered or non-clustered with <code>clustered</code> (SQL Server)</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>The <code>clustered</code> argument is available to configure (non)clustered indexes in SQL Server. It can be used on the <code>@id</code>, <code>@@id</code>, <code>@unique</code>, <code>@@unique</code> and <code>@@index</code> attributes.</p>
<p>As an example, the following model configures the <code>@id</code> to be non-clustered (instead of the clustered default):</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="flex text-fd-muted-foreground items-center gap-2 h-9.5 border-b px-4"><div class="[&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M21.8068 18.2848L13.5528.7565c-.207-.4382-.639-.7273-1.1286-.7541-.5023-.0293-.9523.213-1.2062.6253L2.266 15.1271c-.2773.4518-.2718 1.0091.0158 1.4555l4.3759 6.7786c.2608.4046.7127.6388 1.1823.6388.1332 0 .267-.0188.3987-.0577l12.7019-3.7568c.3891-.1151.7072-.3904.8737-.7553s.1633-.7828-.0075-1.1454zm-1.8481.7519L9.1814 22.2242c-.3292.0975-.6448-.1873-.5756-.5194l3.8501-18.4386c.072-.3448.5486-.3996.699-.0803l7.1288 15.138c.1344.2856-.019.6224-.325.7128z" fill="currentColor" /></svg></div><figcaption class="flex-1 truncate">schema.prisma</figcaption><div class="empty:hidden -me-2"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">model</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Example</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  id    </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> @id</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">clustered</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">false</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  value </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Int</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>This translates to the following SQL commands:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">CREATE</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> TABLE</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> [Example] (</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  id </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">INT</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> NOT NULL</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  value</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> INT</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  CONSTRAINT</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> [Example_pkey] </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">PRIMARY KEY</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> NONCLUSTERED</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (id)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>The default value of <code>clustered</code> for each attribute is as follows:</p>
<div class="relative w-full overflow-auto"><table class="w-full caption-bottom text-sm"><thead class="[&amp;_tr]:border-b"><tr class="border-b transition-colors hover:bg-muted/50 data-[state=selected]:bg-muted"><th class="h-10 px-3 py-4 text-left align-middle font-medium text-foreground-neutral [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] only:text-xl bg-background-neutral-weaker">Attribute</th><th class="h-10 px-3 py-4 text-left align-middle font-medium text-foreground-neutral [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] only:text-xl bg-background-neutral-weaker">Value</th></tr></thead><tbody class="[&amp;_tr:last-child]:border-0"><tr class="border-b transition-colors hover:bg-muted/50 data-[state=selected]:bg-muted"><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"><code>@id</code></td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"><code>true</code></td></tr><tr class="border-b transition-colors hover:bg-muted/50 data-[state=selected]:bg-muted"><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"><code>@@id</code></td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"><code>true</code></td></tr><tr class="border-b transition-colors hover:bg-muted/50 data-[state=selected]:bg-muted"><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"><code>@unique</code></td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"><code>false</code></td></tr><tr class="border-b transition-colors hover:bg-muted/50 data-[state=selected]:bg-muted"><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"><code>@@unique</code></td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"><code>false</code></td></tr><tr class="border-b transition-colors hover:bg-muted/50 data-[state=selected]:bg-muted"><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"><code>@@index</code></td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"><code>false</code></td></tr></tbody></table></div>
<p>A table can have at most one clustered index.</p>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="configuring-the-name-of-indexes-with-map"><a data-card="" href="#configuring-the-name-of-indexes-with-map" class="peer">Configuring the name of indexes with <code>map</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>The <code>map</code> argument allows you to specify a custom name for the index or constraint in the underlying database. This is useful when you want to use a specific naming convention or when the auto-generated name doesn&#x27;t meet your requirements.</p>
<p>The <code>map</code> argument is available on the <code>@id</code>, <code>@@id</code>, <code>@unique</code>, <code>@@unique</code> and <code>@@index</code> attributes.</p>
<p>As an example, the following model configures a custom name for the index on the <code>title</code> field:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="flex text-fd-muted-foreground items-center gap-2 h-9.5 border-b px-4"><div class="[&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M21.8068 18.2848L13.5528.7565c-.207-.4382-.639-.7273-1.1286-.7541-.5023-.0293-.9523.213-1.2062.6253L2.266 15.1271c-.2773.4518-.2718 1.0091.0158 1.4555l4.3759 6.7786c.2608.4046.7127.6388 1.1823.6388.1332 0 .267-.0188.3987-.0577l12.7019-3.7568c.3891-.1151.7072-.3904.8737-.7553s.1633-.7828-.0075-1.1454zm-1.8481.7519L9.1814 22.2242c-.3292.0975-.6448-.1873-.5756-.5194l3.8501-18.4386c.072-.3448.5486-.3996.699-.0803l7.1288 15.138c.1344.2856-.019.6224-.325.7128z" fill="currentColor" /></svg></div><figcaption class="flex-1 truncate">schema.prisma</figcaption><div class="empty:hidden -me-2"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">model</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Post</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  id    </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">    @id</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  title </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">String</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">  @@index</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">([</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">title</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">], </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">map</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;my_custom_index_name&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>This translates to the following SQL command (PostgreSQL example):</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">CREATE</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> INDEX</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> &quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">my_custom_index_name</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&quot; </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">ON</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;Post&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;title&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>Without the <code>map</code> argument, Prisma would generate a default name like <code>Post_title_idx</code>.</p>
<p>The <code>map</code> argument can also be used on unique constraints:</p>

class="[&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M21.8068 18.2848L13.5528.7565c-.207-.4382-.639-.7273-1.1286-.7541-.5023-.0293-.9523.213-1.2062.6253L2.266 15.1271c-.2773.4518-.2718 1.0091.0158 1.4555l4.3759 6.7786c.2608.4046.7127.6388 1.1823.6388.1332 0 .267-.0188.3987-.0577l12.7019-3.7568c.3891-.1151.7072-.3904.8737-.7553s.1633-.7828-.0075-1.1454zm-1.8481.7519L9.1814 22.2242c-.3292.0975-.6448-.1873-.5756-.5194l3.8501-18.4386c.072-.3448.5486-.3996.699-.0803l7.1288 15.138c.1344.2856-.019.6224-.325.7128z" fill="currentColor" /></svg></div><figcaption class="flex-1 truncate">schema.prisma</figcaption><div class="empty:hidden -me-2"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  id    </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">    @id</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  email </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">String</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> @unique</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">map</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;unique_user_email&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>And on composite indexes and constraints:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">model</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Post</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  id        </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">    @id</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  title     </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">String</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  author    </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">String</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  createdAt </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">DateTime</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">  @@index</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">([</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">author</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">createdAt</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">], </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">map</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;posts_author_date_idx&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">  @@unique</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">([</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">title</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">author</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">], </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">map</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;posts_title_author_unique&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="configuring-partial-indexes-with-where"><a data-card="" href="#configuring-partial-indexes-with-where" class="peer">Configuring partial indexes with <code>where</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>The <code>where</code> argument allows you to define <a href="https://www.postgresql.org/docs/current/indexes-partial.html" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">partial indexes</a> (also known as filtered indexes). A partial index only includes rows that match a specified condition, which reduces the index size and improves both write performance and query performance for the indexed subset of data.</p>
<p>The <code>where</code> argument is available on the <code>@unique</code>, <code>@@unique</code> and <code>@@index</code> attributes. It requires the <code>partialIndexes</code> Preview feature.</p>
<div role="alert" class="relative w-full rounded-md border p-4 gap-3 text-sm [&amp;&gt;svg]:left-4 [&amp;&gt;svg]:top-4 [&amp;&gt;svg]:w-5 [&amp;&gt;svg]:h-5 alert-admonition flex items-start [&amp;&gt;i]:mt-0.5 bg-background-ppg text-foreground-ppg border-none [&amp;&gt;svg]:text-foreground-ppg"><i class="fa-duotone fa-solid fa-circle-exclamation"></i><div class="[&amp;&gt;*]:first:mt-0 [&amp;&gt;*]:last:mb-0 [&amp; strong]:text-inherit"><p>Partial indexes are supported on <strong>PostgreSQL</strong>, <strong>SQLite</strong>, <strong>SQL Server</strong>, and <strong>CockroachDB</strong>. They are <strong>not</strong> supported on MySQL.</p></div></div>
<h4 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="enabling-the-partialindexes-preview-feature"><a data-card="" href="#enabling-the-partialindexes-preview-feature" class="peer">Enabling the <code>partialIndexes</code> Preview feature</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h4>
<p>To use partial indexes, add the <code>partialIndexes</code> feature flag to the <code>generator</code> block of your <code>schema.prisma</code> file:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="flex text-fd-muted-foreground items-center gap-2 h-9.5 border-b px-4"><div class="[&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M21.8068 18.2848L13.5528.7565c-.207-.4382-.639-.7273-1.1286-.7541-.5023-.0293-.9523.213-1.2062.6253L2.266 15.1271c-.2773.4518-.2718 1.0091.0158 1.4555l4.3759 6.7786c.2608.4046.7127.6388 1.1823.6388.1332 0 .267-.0188.3987-.0577l12.7019-3.7568c.3891-.1151.7072-.3904.8737-.7553s.1633-.7828-.0075-1.1454zm-1.8481.7519L9.1814 22.2242c-.3292.0975-.6448-.1873-.5756-.5194l3.8501-18.4386c.072-.3448.5486-.3996.699-.0803l7.1288 15.138c.1344.2856-.019.6224-.325.7128z" fill="currentColor" /></svg></div><figcaption class="flex-1 truncate">schema.prisma</figcaption><div class="empty:hidden -me-2"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">generator</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> client</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  provider        </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;prisma-client&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  output          </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;./generated&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  previewFeatures </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> [</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;partialIndexes&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">]</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<h4 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="raw-sql-syntax-with-raw"><a data-card="" href="#raw-sql-syntax-with-raw" class="peer">Raw SQL syntax with <code>raw()</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h4>
<p>You can define a partial index with a raw SQL predicate string using the <code>raw()</code> function. This approach supports any valid SQL <code>WHERE</code> expression that your database accepts:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="flex text-fd-muted-foreground items-center gap-2 h-9.5 border-b px-4"><div class="[&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M21.8068 18.2848L13.5528.7565c-.207-.4382-.639-.7273-1.1286-.7541-.5023-.0293-.9523.213-1.2062.6253L2.266 15.1271c-.2773.4518-.2718 1.0091.0158 1.4555l4.3759 6.7786c.2608.4046.7127.6388 1.1823.6388.1332 0 .267-.0188.3987-.0577l12.7019-3.7568c.3891-.1151.7072-.3904.8737-.7553s.1633-.7828-.0075-1.1454zm-1.8481.7519L9.1814 22.2242c-.3292.0975-.6448-.1873-.5756-.5194l3.8501-18.4386c.072-.3448.5486-.3996.699-.0803l7.1288 15.138c.1344.2856-.019.6224-.325.7128z" fill="currentColor" /></svg></div><figcaption class="flex-1
