disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">model</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> User</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  id        </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">       @id</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  email     </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">String</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  status    </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">String</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  deletedAt </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">DateTime</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">?</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">  @@unique</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">([</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">email</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">], </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">where</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">raw</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;status</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> &#x27;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">active</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&#x27;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">))</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">  @@index</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">([</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">email</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">], </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">where</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">raw</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;\&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">deletedAt</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">\</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> IS</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> NULL&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">))</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>This generates SQL like:</p>
<p><strong>PostgreSQL:</strong></p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">CREATE</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> UNIQUE INDEX</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> &quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">User_email_key</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&quot; </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">ON</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;User&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;email&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">WHERE</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">status</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &#x27;active&#x27;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">CREATE</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> INDEX</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> &quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">User_email_idx</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&quot; </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">ON</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;User&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;email&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">WHERE</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;deletedAt&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> IS</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> NULL</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p><strong>SQLite:</strong></p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">CREATE</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> UNIQUE INDEX</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> &quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">User_email_key</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&quot; </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">ON</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;User&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;email&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">WHERE</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> status</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &#x27;active&#x27;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">CREATE</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> INDEX</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> &quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">User_email_idx</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&quot; </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">ON</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;User&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;email&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">WHERE</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;deletedAt&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> IS</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> NULL</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p><strong>SQL Server:</strong></p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">CREATE</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> UNIQUE</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> NONCLUSTERED</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> INDEX</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> [User_email_key] </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">ON</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> [dbo].[User]([email]) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">WHERE</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> ([status]</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&#x27;active&#x27;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">CREATE</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> NONCLUSTERED</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> INDEX</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> [User_email_idx] </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">ON</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> [dbo].[User]([email]) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">WHERE</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> ([deletedAt] </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">IS</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> NULL</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>The <code>raw()</code> syntax can be used with any SQL expression your database supports, making it the most flexible option.</p>
<h4 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="object-literal-syntax-type-safe-alternative"><a data-card="" href="#object-literal-syntax-type-safe-alternative" class="peer">Object literal syntax (type-safe alternative)</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h4>
<p>You can also define partial indexes using an object literal syntax, which provides type-safety by validating field names and value types against your Prisma schema:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="flex text-fd-muted-foreground items-center gap-2 h-9.5 border-b px-4"><div class="[&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M21.8068 18.2848L13.5528.7565c-.207-.4382-.639-.7273-1.1286-.7541-.5023-.0293-.9523.213-1.2062.6253L2.266 15.1271c-.2773.4518-.2718 1.0091.0158 1.4555l4.3759 6.7786c.2608.4046.7127.6388 1.1823.6388.1332 0 .267-.0188.3987-.0577l12.7019-3.7568c.3891-.1151.7072-.3904.8737-.7553s.1633-.7828-.0075-1.1454zm-1.8481.7519L9.1814 22.2242c-.3292.0975-.6448-.1873-.5756-.5194l3.8501-18.4386c.072-.3448.5486-.3996.699-.0803l7.1288 15.138c.1344.2856-.019.6224-.325.7128z" fill="currentColor" /></svg></div><figcaption class="flex-1 truncate">schema.prisma</figcaption><div class="empty:hidden -me-2"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">model</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Post</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  id        </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">      @id</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  title     </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">String</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  published </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Boolean</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">  @@index</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">([</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">title</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">], </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">where</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: { </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">published</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">true</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> })</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">  @@unique</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">([</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">title</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">], </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">where</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: { </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">published</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">true</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> })</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>The object literal syntax supports the following value types:</p>
<div class="relative w-full overflow-auto"><table class="w-full caption-bottom text-sm"><thead class="[&amp;_tr]:border-b"><tr class="border-b transition-colors hover:bg-muted/50 data-[state=selected]:bg-muted"><th class="h-10 px-3 py-4 text-left align-middle font-medium text-foreground-neutral [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] only:text-xl bg-background-neutral-weaker">Value type</th><th class="h-10 px-3 py-4 text-left align-middle font-medium text-foreground-neutral [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] only:text-xl bg-background-neutral-weaker">Example</th><th class="h-10 px-3 py-4 text-left align-middle font-medium text-foreground-neutral [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] only:text-xl bg-background-neutral-weaker">Notes</th></tr></thead><tbody class="[&amp;_tr:last-child]:border-0"><tr class="border-b transition-colors hover:bg-muted/50 data-[state=selected]:bg-muted"><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"><code>Boolean</code></td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"><code>{ active: true }</code>, <code>{ deleted: false }</code></td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default">For <code>Boolean</code> fields</td></tr><tr class="border-b transition-colors hover:bg-muted/50 data-[state=selected]:bg-muted"><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"><code>String</code></td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"><code>{ status: &quot;active&quot; }</code></td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default">For <code>String</code>, <code>DateTime</code>, and <code>Enum</code> fields</td></tr><tr class="border-b transition-colors hover:bg-muted/50 data-[state=selected]:bg-muted"><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"><code>Number</code></td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"><code>{ priority: 1 }</code>, <code>{ score: 1.5 }</code></td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default">For <code>Int</code>, <code>BigInt</code>, <code>Float</code>, and <code>Decimal</code> fields</td></tr><tr class="border-b transition-colors hover:bg-muted/50 data-[state=selected]:bg-muted"><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"><code>null</code></td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"><code>{ deletedAt: null }</code></td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default">Translates to <code>IS NULL</code>. Works with any nullable field</td></tr><tr class="border-b transition-colors hover:bg-muted/50 data-[state=selected]:bg-muted"><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"><code>{ not: value }</code></td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default"><code>{ deletedAt: { not: null } }</code></td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default">Negation. Translates to <code>IS NOT NULL</code> or <code>!= value</code></td></tr></tbody></table></div>
<p>You can combine multiple conditions in a single object:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="flex text-fd-muted-foreground items-center gap-2 h-9.5 border-b px-4"><div class="[&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M21.8068 18.2848L13.5528.7565c-.207-.4382-.639-.7273-1.1286-.7541-.5023-.0293-.9523.213-1.2062.6253L2.266 15.1271c-.2773.4518-.2718 1.0091.0158 1.4555l4.3759 6.7786c.2608.4046.7127.6388 1.1823.6388.1332 0 .267-.0188.3987-.0577l12.7019-3.7568c.3891-.1151.7072-.3904.8737-.7553s.1633-.7828-.0075-1.1454zm-1.8481.7519L9.1814 22.2242c-.3292.0975-.6448-.1873-.5756-.5194l3.8501-18.4386c.072-.3448.5486-.3996.699-.0803l7.1288 15.138c.1344.2856-.019.6224-.325.7128z" fill="currentColor" /></svg></div><figcaption class="flex-1 truncate">schema.prisma</figcaption><div class="empty:hidden -me-2"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">model</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> User</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  id        </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">       @id</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  email     </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">String</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  active    </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Boolean</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  deletedAt </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">DateTime</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">?</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">  @@unique</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">([</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">email</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">], </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">where</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: { </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">active</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">true</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">deletedAt</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">null</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> })</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<div role="alert" class="relative w-full rounded-md border p-4 gap-3 text-sm [&amp;&gt;svg]:left-4 [&amp;&gt;svg]:top-4 [&amp;&gt;svg]:w-5 [&amp;&gt;svg]:h-5 alert-admonition flex items-start [&amp;&gt;i]:mt-0.5 bg-background-ppg text-foreground-ppg border-none [&amp;&gt;svg]:text-foreground-ppg"><i class="fa-duotone fa-solid fa-circle-exclamation"></i><div class="[&amp;&gt;*]:first:mt-0 [&amp;&gt;*]:last:mb-0 [&amp; strong]:text-inherit"><p>The object literal syntax validates field types. For example, you cannot use a <code>Boolean</code> value for a <code>String</code> field. For fields with types that are not supported by the object syntax (such as <code>Unsupported</code> or composite types), use <code>raw()</code> instead.</p></div></div>
<h4 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="using-where-with-other-index-arguments"><a data-card="" href="#using-where-with-other-index-arguments" class="peer">Using <code>where</code> with other index arguments</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h4>
<p>The <code>where</code> argument can be combined with other index arguments such as <code>name</code> and <code>map</code>:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="flex text-fd-muted-foreground items-center gap-2 h-9.5 border-b px-4"><div class="[&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M21.8068 18.2848L13.5528.7565c-.207-.4382-.639-.7273-1.1286-.7541-.5023-.0293-.9523.213-1.2062.6253L2.266 15.1271c-.2773.4518-.2718 1.0091.0158 1.4555l4.3759 6.7786c.2608.4046.7127.6388 1.1823.6388.1332 0 .267-.0188.3987-.0577l12.7019-3.7568c.3891-.1151.7072-.3904.8737-.7553s.1633-.7828-.0075-1.1454zm-1.8481.7519L9.1814 22.2242c-.3292.0975-.6448-.1873-.5756-.5194l3.8501-18.4386c.072-.3448.5486-.3996.699-.0803l7.1288 15.138c.1344.2856-.019.6224-.325.7128z" fill="currentColor" /></svg></div><figcaption class="flex-1 truncate">schema.prisma</figcaption><div class="empty:hidden -me-2"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  id     </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">    @id</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  email  </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">String</span></span>

<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">  @@unique</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">([</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">email</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">], </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">name</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;email_active_unique&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">map</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;idx_email_active&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">where</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">raw</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;status</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> &#x27;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">active</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&#x27;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">))</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<h4 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="database-specific-behavior"><a data-card="" href="#database-specific-behavior" class="peer">Database-specific behavior</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h4>
<div class="relative w-full overflow-auto"><table class="w-full caption-bottom text-sm"><thead class="[&amp;_tr]:border-b"><tr class="border-b transition-colors hover:bg-muted/50 text-foreground-neutral [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] only:text-xl bg-background-neutral-weaker">Notes</th></tr></thead><tbody py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default">Full support</td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default">Full support</td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default">Create only</td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default">Not supported</td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 hover:bg-muted/50 data-[state=selected]:bg-muted"><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default">MySQL</td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default">Not supported</td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default">Not supported</td><td class="px-3 py-4 align-middle [&amp;:has([role=checkbox])]:pr-0 [&amp;&gt;[role=checkbox]]:translate-y-[2px] bg-background-default">Partial indexes are not supported by the database</td></tr></tbody></table></div>
<div role="alert" class="relative w-full rounded-md border p-4 gap-3 text-sm [&amp;&gt;svg]:left-4 [&amp;&gt;svg]:top-4 [&amp;&gt;svg]:w-5 [&amp;&gt;svg]:h-5 alert-admonition flex items-start [&amp;&gt;i]:mt-0.5 bg-background-warning border-none text-foreground-warning [&amp;&gt;svg]:text-foreground-warning"><i class="fa-duotone fa-solid fa-circle-exclamation"></i><div class="[&amp;&gt;*]:first:mt-0 [&amp;&gt;*]:last:mb-0 [&amp; strong]:text-inherit"><p><strong>CockroachDB limitation</strong>: CockroachDB supports creating partial indexes, but it cannot introspect the predicate text from existing indexes. This means that after initial creation, modifications to the <code>where</code> clause (adding, changing, or removing a predicate) will not be detected by Prisma Migrate. The differ skips predicate comparison for CockroachDB to prevent false-positive migrations.</p></div></div>
<h4 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="introspection"><a data-card="" href="#introspection" class="peer">Introspection</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h4>
<p>When you run <code>prisma db pull</code> on a database that contains partial indexes, Prisma ORM will:</p>
<ol>
<li>Automatically add <code>&quot;partialIndexes&quot;</code> to the <code>previewFeatures</code> list in your generator block</li>
<li>Represent the partial index predicate using the <code>raw()</code> syntax with the database&#x27;s normalized form of the SQL expression</li>
</ol>
<p>For example, a PostgreSQL partial unique index on a single field will be introspected as:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="flex text-fd-muted-foreground items-center gap-2 h-9.5 border-b px-4"><div class="[&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M21.8068 18.2848L13.5528.7565c-.207-.4382-.639-.7273-1.1286-.7541-.5023-.0293-.9523.213-1.2062.6253L2.266 15.1271c-.2773.4518-.2718 1.0091.0158 1.4555l4.3759 6.7786c.2608.4046.7127.6388 1.1823.6388.1332 0 .267-.0188.3987-.0577l12.7019-3.7568c.3891-.1151.7072-.3904.8737-.7553s.1633-.7828-.0075-1.1454zm-1.8481.7519L9.1814 22.2242c-.3292.0975-.6448-.1873-.5756-.5194l3.8501-18.4386c.072-.3448.5486-.3996.699-.0803l7.1288 15.138c.1344.2856-.019.6224-.325.7128z" fill="currentColor" /></svg></div><figcaption class="flex-1 truncate">schema.prisma</figcaption><div class="empty:hidden -me-2"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">model</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> User</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  id     </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">    @id</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  email  </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">String</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> @unique</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">where</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">raw</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">status</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> &#x27;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">active</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&#x27;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">::text</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">))</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  status </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">String</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<div role="alert" class="relative w-full rounded-md border p-4 gap-3 text-sm [&amp;&gt;svg]:left-4 [&amp;&gt;svg]:top-4 [&amp;&gt;svg]:w-5 [&amp;&gt;svg]:h-5 alert-admonition flex items-start [&amp;&gt;i]:mt-0.5 bg-background-ppg text-foreground-ppg border-none [&amp;&gt;svg]:text-foreground-ppg"><i class="fa-duotone fa-solid fa-circle-exclamation"></i><div class="[&amp;&gt;*]:first:mt-0 [&amp;&gt;*]:last:mb-0 [&amp; strong]:text-inherit"><p>The introspected <code>raw()</code> string reflects the database&#x27;s normalized form of the SQL expression, which may differ from what you originally wrote. For example, PostgreSQL adds parentheses and explicit type casts (e.g., <code>&#x27;active&#x27;::text</code>), SQL Server wraps column names in brackets and adds parentheses (e.g., <code>([status]=&#x27;active&#x27;)</code>), while SQLite generally preserves the original expression as-is.</p></div></div>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="full-text-indexes-mysql-and-mongodb"><a data-card="" href="#full-text-indexes-mysql-and-mongodb" class="peer">Full text indexes (MySQL and MongoDB)</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>The <code>fullTextIndex</code> preview feature provides support for introspection and migration of full text indexes in MySQL and MongoDB. This can be configured using the <code>@@fulltext</code> attribute. Existing full text indexes in the database are added to your Prisma schema after introspecting with <code>db pull</code>, and new full text indexes added in the Prisma schema are created in the database when using Prisma Migrate.</p>
<div role="alert" class="relative w-full rounded-md border p-4 gap-3 text-sm [&amp;&gt;svg]:left-4 [&amp;&gt;svg]:top-4 [&amp;&gt;svg]:w-5 [&amp;&gt;svg]:h-5 alert-admonition flex items-start [&amp;&gt;i]:mt-0.5 bg-background-warning border-none text-foreground-warning [&amp;&gt;svg]:text-foreground-warning"><i class="fa-duotone fa-solid fa-circle-exclamation"></i><div class="[&amp;&gt;*]:first:mt-0 [&amp;&gt;*]:last:mb-0 [&amp; strong]:text-inherit"><p>For now we do not enable the full text search commands in Prisma Client for MongoDB; the progress can be followed in the <a href="https://github.com/prisma/prisma/issues/9413" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">MongoDB</a> issue.</p></div></div>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="enabling-the-fulltextindex-preview-feature"><a data-card="" href="#enabling-the-fulltextindex-preview-feature" class="peer">Enabling the <code>fullTextIndex</code> preview feature</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>To enable the <code>fullTextIndex</code> preview feature, add the <code>fullTextIndex</code> feature flag to the <code>generator</code> block of the <code>schema.prisma</code> file:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  provider        </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;prisma-client&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  output          </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;./generated&quot;</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="examples"><a data-card="" href="#examples" class="peer">Examples</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>The following example demonstrates adding a <code>@@fulltext</code> index to the <code>title</code> and <code>content</code> fields of a <code>Post</code> model:</p>

1.0091.0158 1.4555l4.3759 6.7786c.2608.4046.7127.6388 1.1823.6388.1332 0 .267-.0188.3987-.0577l12.7019-3.7568c.3891-.1151.7072-.3904.8737-.7553s.1633-.7828-.0075-1.1454zm-1.8481.7519L9.1814 <p>On MongoDB, you can use the <code>@@fulltext</code> index attribute (via the <code>fullTextIndex</code> preview feature) with the <code>sort</code> argument to add fields to your full-text index in ascending or descending order. The following example adds a <code>@@fulltext</code> index to the <code>title</code> and <code>content</code> fields of the <code>Post</code> model, and sorts the <code>title</code> field in descending order:</p>

<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  title   </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">String</span></span>
